msg:Before I checked in, I thought it was a star-rated resort hotel, at least four-star, but I didn't expect to live in a "resort hotel" whose service level was not as good as that of a business hotel that costs 250 yuan a night!
1. For temporarily booked hotels, Ctrip booking reminder: medium and high-risk areas are checked in with the nucleic acid result, and low-risk areas are checked in with a green code. As a result, I arrived at the front desk to check in at 6 o'clock in the evening and informed that all guests who check in need 24-hour nucleic acid! Then he directed us to the local police station for nucleic acid testing! When we went to the police station to do the nucleic acid test, the police told us that there is no need for nucleic acid testing in low-risk areas to check in. The nucleic acid point is specially opened for passengers from medium and high-risk areas! So, why do hotels ignore national policies to increase epidemic prevention policies at will? ! In addition, the hotel has such a request, why did not call in advance to inform? Why take it for granted that I would know? ! Is it fun for me to run around with two kids? !
2. When we finished the nucleic acid check-in at 7:30 p.m., I asked the front desk customer service if we could check out late tomorrow because we checked in so late, and the answer was "no"!
3. Regarding the room, to be honest, the hygiene is ok, but the most unbearable thing is the noise! There is a big road outside the room window, and the sound of rumbling trucks passing by all night caused us to wake up and fall asleep, with a headache! As a resort hotel, we were woken up by a large truck, which is unbelievable! When I checked in yesterday, the uncle who stayed in front of me also upgraded the lake view room for free. I thought at the time, forget it, I'm not greedy, I don't need to look at the lake view, so there is no such thing as an upgrade, but , the sister at the front desk, even if you see me with two children, you are not willing to upgrade me, should you inform me in advance that the room is so noisy? I may consider adding money to upgrade the holiday? It doesn't even think about customers at all! No sense of service at all! During the epidemic, there were only a dozen rooms in the entire hotel (I saw the list when I had breakfast), and there were a lot of rooms. You upgraded someone else's uncle, but you didn't want to upgrade me. The only thing that can explain is that you look at me. dislike; despise! It's so bad, just don't do it!
4. The management at the front desk of the hot spring is poor, the gate is always open, whether to buy a ticket when entering the hot spring, how many people go in depends purely on self-consciousness.
5. I used to eat breakfast at Hilton. Today is the first day I went to the 2nd floor of the hotel to eat. This breakfast is also the most shabby and monotonous breakfast I have ever seen. Order, there are beef offal noodles, beef balls, 2 kinds of buns to choose from, corn, boiled egg buffet, watermelon slices buffet, tea... No, my son said that the noodles are unpalatable, the packaging is the kind that can only be filled. Fill your stomach.
6. Seeing that I am carrying children, I did not provide children's toothbrushes and slippers...

Destroy it, this kind of hotel should not be listed as a "resort hotel"!
